   231	   * @param {number|string} duration
   232	   */
   233	  result(passed, failed, skipped, duration, failedHooks = 0) {
   234	    let style = colors.bgGreen
   235	    let msg = ` ${passed || 0} passed`
   236	    let status = style.bold('  OK ')
   237	    if (failed) {
   238	      style = style.bgRed
   239	      status = style.bold('  FAIL ')
   240	      msg += `, ${failed} failed`
   241	    }
   242	
   243	    if (failedHooks > 0) {
   244	      style = style.bgRed
   245	      status = style.bold('  FAIL ')
   246	      msg += `, ${failedHooks} failedHooks`
   247	    }
   248	    status += style.grey(' |')
   249	
   250	    if (skipped) {
   251	      if (!failed) style = style.bgYellow
   252	      msg += `, ${skipped} skipped`
   253	    }
   254	    msg += '  '
   255	    print(status + style(msg) + colors.grey(` // ${duration}`))
   256	  },
   257	}
   258	
   259	function print(...msg) {
   260	  if (outputProcess) {
   261	    msg.unshift(outputProcess)
   262	  }
   263	  if (!newline) {
   264	    console.log()
   265	    newline = true
   266	  }
   267	
   268	  console.log.apply(this, msg)
   269	}
   270	
   271	function truncate(msg, gap = 0) {
   272	  if (msg.indexOf('\n') > 0 || outputLevel >= 3) {
   273	    return msg // don't cut multi line steps or on verbose log level
   274	  }
   275	  const width = (process.stdout.columns || 200) - gap - 4
   276	  if (msg.length > width) {
   277	    msg = msg.substr(0, width - 1) + figures.ellipsis
   278	  }
   279	  return msg
   280	}

    15	 * CodeceptJS runner

    17	class Codecept {
    18	  /**
    19	   * Create CodeceptJS runner.
    20	   * Config and options should be passed
    21	   *
    22	   * @param {*} config
    23	   * @param {*} opts
    24	   */
    25	  constructor(config, opts) {
    26	    this.config = Config.create(config)
    27	    this.opts = opts
    28	    this.testFiles = new Array(0)
    29	    this.requireModules(config.require)
    30	  }
    31	
    32	  /**
    33	   * Require modules before codeceptjs running
    34	   *
    35	   * @param {string[]} requiringModules
    36	   */
    37	  requireModules(requiringModules) {
    38	    if (requiringModules) {
    39	      requiringModules.forEach(requiredModule => {
    40	        const isLocalFile = existsSync(requiredModule) || existsSync(`${requiredModule}.js`)
    41	        if (isLocalFile) {
    42	          requiredModule = resolve(requiredModule)
    43	        }
    44	        require(requiredModule)
    45	      })
    46	    }
    47	  }
    48	
    49	  /**
    50	   * Initialize CodeceptJS at specific directory.
    51	   * If async initialization is required, pass callback as second parameter.
    52	   *
    53	   * @param {string} dir
    54	   */
    55	  init(dir) {
    56	    this.initGlobals(dir)
    57	    // initializing listeners
    58	    container.create(this.config, this.opts)
    59	    this.runHooks()
    60	  }

'use strict';

/**
 * Predefined patterns for masking sensitive data
 * Each pattern contains a name, regex, and mask string
 */

// Reusable regex components
const SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN = '([^"\\s\\r\\n]+)';
const OBFUSCATED_STRING = '****';

/**
 * Creates a pattern object for sensitive data masking
 * @param {string} name - Human readable name for the pattern
 * @param {RegExp} regex - Regular expression to match sensitive data
 * @param {string} mask - Replacement string for matched data
 * @returns {Object} Pattern object
 */
function createPattern(name, regex, mask) {
    return { name, regex, mask };
}

/**
 * Predefined patterns for common sensitive data types
 */
const PREDEFINED_PATTERNS = [
    createPattern(
        'Authorization Header',
        new RegExp(`"Authorization"\\s*:\\s*"Bearer\\s+${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"Authorization": "Bearer ${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Authorization Header in cURL',
        new RegExp(`"Authorization\\s*Bearer\\s+${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"Authorization Bearer ${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'API Key',
        new RegExp(`"api[-_]?key"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"api-key": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Access Token',
        new RegExp(`"access[-_]?token"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"access-token": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Refresh Token',
        new RegExp(`"refresh[-_]?token"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"refresh-token": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Client ID',
        new RegExp(`"client[-_]?id"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"client-id": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'ID Token',
        new RegExp(`"id[-_]?token"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"id-token": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Client Secret',
        new RegExp(`"client[-_]?secret"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"client-secret": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Token',
        new RegExp(`"token"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"token": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Password',
        new RegExp(`"password"\\s*:\\s*"${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"password": "${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
    createPattern(
        'Basic Authorization',
        new RegExp(`"Authorization"\\s*:\\s*"Basic\\s+${SENSITIVE_VALUE_PATTERN}"`, 'gi'),
        `"Authorization": "Basic ${OBFUSCATED_STRING}"`
    ),
];

/**
 * Custom error for invalid input
 */
class InvalidInputError extends Error {
    constructor(message) {
        super(message);
        this.name = 'InvalidInputError';
    }
}

/**
 * Validates input parameter
 * @param {*} input - The input to validate
 * @throws {InvalidInputError} If input is invalid
 */
function validateInput(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') {
        throw new InvalidInputError('Input must be a valid string');
    }
    
    if (input.trim().length === 0) {
        throw new InvalidInputError('Input cannot be empty or whitespace only');
    }
}

/**
 * Masks sensitive data in a given string using predefined and custom patterns.
 * @param {string} input - The input string that may contain sensitive data
 * @param {Array} customPatterns - Optional array of custom masking patterns
 * @returns {string} A new string with sensitive data masked
 * @throws {InvalidInputError} If input is not a valid string
 */
function maskSensitiveData(input, customPatterns = []) {
    validateInput(input);
    
    // Combine predefined patterns with custom patterns
    const patterns = [...PREDEFINED_PATTERNS, ...customPatterns];

    let maskedString = input;

    // Apply each pattern to mask sensitive data
    patterns.forEach

     1	const { maskSensitiveData } = require('invisi-data')
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * Mask sensitive data utility for CodeceptJS
     5	 * Supports both boolean and object configuration formats
     6	 *
     7	 * @param {string} input - The string to mask
     8	 * @param {boolean|object} config - Masking configuration
     9	 * @returns {string} - Masked string
    10	 */
    11	function maskData(input, config) {
    12	  if (!config) {
    13	    return input
    14	  }
    15	
    16	  // Handle boolean config (backward compatibility)
    17	  if (typeof config === 'boolean' && config === true) {
    18	    return maskSensitiveData(input)
    19	  }
    20	
    21	  // Handle object config with custom patterns
    22	  if (typeof config === 'object' && config.enabled === true) {
    23	    const customPatterns = config.patterns || []
    24	    return maskSensitiveData(input, customPatterns)
    25	  }
    26	
    27	  return input
    28	}
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * Check if masking is enabled based on global configuration
    32	 *
    33	 * @returns {boolean|object} - Current masking configuration
    34	 */
    35	function getMaskConfig() {
    36	  return global.maskSensitiveData || false
    37	}
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Check if data should be masked
    41	 *
    42	 * @returns {boolean} - True if masking is enabled
    43	 */
    44	function shouldMaskData() {
    45	  const config = getMaskConfig()
    46	  return config === true || (typeof config === 'object' && config.enabled === true)
    47	}
    48	
    49	module.exports = {
    50	  maskData,
    51	  getMaskConfig,
    52	  shouldMaskData,
    53	}

   110	  step(step) {
   111	    if (outputLevel === 0) return
   112	    if (!step) return
   113	    // Avoid to print non-gherkin steps, when gherkin is running for --steps mode
   114	    if (outputLevel === 1) {
   115	      if (typeof step === 'object' && step.hasBDDAncestor()) {
   116	        return
   117	      }
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    let stepLine = step.toCliStyled ? step.toCliStyled() : step.toString()
   121	    if (step.metaStep && outputLevel >= 1) {
   122	      // this.stepShift += 2;
   123	      stepLine = colors.dim(truncate(stepLine, this.spaceShift))
   124	    }
   125	    if (step.comment) {
   126	      stepLine += colors.grey(step.comment.split('\n').join('\n' + ' '.repeat(4)))
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    const _stepLine = shouldMaskData() ? maskData(stepLine, getMaskConfig()) : stepLine
   130	    print(' '.repeat(this.stepShift), truncate(_stepLine, this.spaceShift))
   131	  },

   175	  scenario: {
   176	    /**
   177	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   178	     */
   179	
   180	    started(test) {
   181	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   182	      print(`  ${colors.dim.bold('Scenario()')}`)
   183	    },
   184	
   185	    /**
   186	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   187	     */
   188	    passed(test) {
   189	      print(`  ${colors.green.bold(`${figures.tick} OK`)} ${colors.grey(`in ${test.duration}ms`)}`)
   190	      print()
   191	    },
   192	    /**
   193	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   194	     */
   195	    failed(test) {
   196	      print(`  ${colors.red.bold(`${figures.cross} FAILED`)} ${colors.grey(`in ${test.duration}ms`)}`)
   197	      print()
   198	    },
   199	  },
   200	
   201	  hook: {
   202	    started(hook) {
   203	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   204	      print(`  ${colors.dim.bold(hook.toCode())}`)
   205	    },
   206	    passed(hook) {
   207	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   208	      print()
   209	    },
   210	    failed(hook) {
   211	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   212	      print(`  ${colors.red.bold(hook.toCode())}`)
   213	    },
   214	  },
   215	
   216	  /**
   217	   *
   218	   * Print a text in console log
   219	   * @param {string} message
   220	   * @param {string} [color]
   221	   */
   222	  say(message, color = 'cyan') {
   223	    if (colors[color] === undefined) {
   224	      color = 'cyan'
   225	    }
   226	    if (outputLevel >= 1) print(`   ${colors[color].bold(message)}`)
   227	  },
   228	
   229	  /**
   230	   * @param {number} passed
   231	   * @param {number} failed
   232	   * @param {number} skipped
   233	   * @param {number|string} duration
   234	   */
   235	  result(passed, failed, skipped, duration, failedHooks = 0) {
   236	    let style = colors.bgGreen
   237	    let msg = ` ${passed || 0} passed`
   238	    let status = style.bold('  OK ')
   239	    if (failed) {
   240	      style = style.bgRed

## 🎨 Advanced Usage

### Custom Patterns

Create your own masking patterns for domain-specific sensitive data:

```javascript
import { maskSensitiveData, createPattern } from 'invisi-data';

// Create custom patterns
const customPatterns = [
    createPattern(
        'Database Password',
        /"db_password"\s*:\s*"([^"]+)"/gi,
        '"db_password": "****"'
    ),
    createPattern(
        'SSH Private Key',
        /"ssh_key"\s*:\s*"([^"]+)"/gi,
        '"ssh_key": "****"'
    )
];

const config = JSON.stringify({
    database: {
        host: "localhost",
        db_password: "super_secret_db_pass"
    },
    deployment: {
        ssh_key: "-----BEGIN PRIVATE KEY-----\nMIIEvQ...",
        api_key: "prod_api_key_123"
    }
});

const masked = maskSensitiveData(config, customPatterns);
console.log(masked);
```

### Real-World Scenarios

#### HTTP Request Logging
```javascript
const httpLog = `POST /api/auth - Headers: {"Authorization": "Bearer eyJhbGci...", "Content-Type": "application/json"} - Body: {"username": "user", "password": "secret123"}`;

const sanitizedLog = maskSensitiveData(httpLog);
console.log(sanitizedLog);
// Output: POST /api/auth - Headers: {"Authorization": "Bearer ****", "Content-Type": "application/json"} - Body: {"username": "user", "password": "****"}
```

const appConfig = {
    server: { port: 3000, host: "localhost" },

        "api-key": "prod_api_key_abc123"
    },

const output = require('/testbed/lib/output');
const { createPattern } = require('/testbed/node_modules/invisi-data');

function capture(fn) {
  const original = console.log;
  const lines = [];
  console.log = (...args) => lines.push(args.join(' '));
  try { fn(); } finally { console.log = original; }
  return lines.join('\n');
}

output.level(3);
global.maskSensitiveData = {
  enabled: true,
  patterns: [
    createPattern('Email', /"email"\s*:\s*"([^"]+)"/gi, '"email": "****"'),
  ],
};

const msg = 'payload {"password":"secret123","email":"user@example.com"}';
const out = capture(() => {
  output.debug(msg);
  output.log(msg);
  output.error(msg);
});
console.log(out);
if (out.includes('secret123') || out.includes('user@example.com')) {
  console.error('Sensitive data leaked');
  process.exit(1);
}
console.log('OK');
NODE

str_replace_editor create /testbed/lib/mask_data.js --file_text 'const { maskSensitiveData } = require('"'"'invisi-data'"'"')

/**
 * Mask sensitive data utility for CodeceptJS.
 *
 * Supports backward-compatible boolean configuration and object configuration
 * with custom invisi-data patterns:
 *
 * maskSensitiveData: true
 * maskSensitiveData: { enabled: true, patterns: [{ regex: /.../, mask: '"'"'...'"'"' }] }
 *
 * @param {string} input
 * @param {boolean|object} config
 * @returns {string}
 */
function maskData(input, config = getMaskConfig()) {
  if (!shouldMaskData(config) || typeof input !== '"'"'string'"'"' || input.trim().length === 0) {
    return input
  }

  if (config === true) {
    return maskSensitiveData(input)
  }

  return maskSensitiveData(input, normalizePatterns(config.patterns || []))
}

/**
 * @returns {boolean|object}
 */
function getMaskConfig() {
  return global.maskSensitiveData || false
}

/**
 * @param {boolean|object} config
 * @returns {boolean}
 */
function shouldMaskData(config = getMaskConfig()) {
  return config === true || (typeof config === '"'"'object'"'"' && config !== null && config.enabled !== false)
}

/**
 * Convert string regex definitions to RegExp objects while keeping existing
 * RegExp-based invisi-data patterns intact.
 *
 * @param {Array} patterns
 * @returns {Array}
 */
function normalizePatterns(patterns) {
  if (!Array.isArray(patterns)) return []

  return patterns.map(pattern => {
    if (!pattern || typeof pattern !== '"'"'object'"'"' || pattern.regex instanceof RegExp) return pattern
    if (typeof pattern.regex !== '"'"'string'"'"') return pattern

    return {
      ...pattern,
      regex: stringToRegExp(pattern.regex),
    }
  })
}

/**
 * Accept either a plain regex source or JavaScript-like /source/flags notation.
 *
 * @param {string} value
 * @returns {RegExp|string}
 */
function stringToRegExp(value) {
  const match = value.match(/^\/(.*)\/([a-z]*)$/i)
  if (!match) return new RegExp(value, '"'"'g'"'"')

  return new RegExp(match[1], match[2])
}

module.exports = {
  maskData,
  getMaskConfig,
  shouldMaskData,
  normalizePatterns,
}

   132	
   133	  /** @namespace */
   134	  suite: {
   135	    /**
   136	     * @param {Mocha.Suite} suite
   137	     */
   138	    started: suite => {
   139	      if (!suite.title) return
   140	      print(`${colors.bold(suite.title)} --`)
   141	      if (suite.file && outputLevel >= 1) print(colors.underline.grey(suite.file))
   142	      if (suite.comment) print(suite.comment)
   143	    },
   144	  },
   145	
   146	  /** @namespace */
   147	  test: {
   148	    /**
   149	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   150	     */
   151	    started(test) {
   152	      print(`  ${colors.magenta.bold(test.title)}`)
   153	    },
   154	    /**
   155	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   156	     */
   157	    passed(test) {
   158	      print(`  ${colors.green.bold(figures.tick)} ${test.title} ${colors.grey(`in ${test.duration}ms`)}`)
   159	    },
   160	    /**
   161	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   162	     */
   163	    failed(test) {
   164	      print(`  ${colors.red.bold(figures.cross)} ${test.title} ${colors.grey(`in ${test.duration}ms`)}`)
   165	    },
   166	    /**
   167	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   168	     */
   169	    skipped(test) {
   170	      print(`  ${colors.yellow.bold('S')} ${test.title}`)
   171	    },
   172	  },
   173	
   174	  /** @namespace */
   175	  scenario: {
   176	    /**
   177	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   178	     */
   179	
   180	    started(test) {
   181	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   182	      print(`  ${colors.dim.bold('Scenario()')}`)
   183	    },
   184	
   185	    /**
   186	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   187	     */
   188	    passed(test) {
   189	      print(`  ${colors.green.bold(`${figures.tick} OK`)} ${colors.grey(`in ${test.duration}ms`)}`)
   190	      print()
   191	    },
   192	    /**
   193	     * @param {Mocha.Test} test
   194	     */
   195	    failed(test) {
   196	      print(`  ${colors.red.bold(`${figures.cross} FAILED`)} ${colors.grey(`in ${test.duration}ms`)}`)
   197	      print()
   198	    },
   199	  },
   200	
   201	  hook: {
   202	    started(hook) {
   203	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   204	      print(`  ${colors.dim.bold(hook.toCode())}`)
   205	    },
   206	    passed(hook) {
   207	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   208	      print()
   209	    },
   210	    failed(hook) {
   211	      if (outputLevel < 1) return
   212	      print(`  ${colors.red.bold(hook.toCode())}`)
   213	    },
   214	  },
   215	
   216	  /**
   217	   *
   218	   * Print a text in console log
   219	   * @param {string} message
   220	   * @param {string} [color]
   221	   */
   222	  say(message, color = 'cyan') {
   223	    if (colors[color] === undefined) {
   224	      color = 'cyan'
   225	    }
   226	    if (outputLevel >= 1) print(`   ${colors[color].bold(message)}`)
   227	  },
   228	
   229	  /**
   230	   * @param {number} passed
   231	   * @param {number} failed
   232	   * @param {number} skipped
   233	   * @param {number|string} duration
   234	   */
   235	  result(passed, failed, skipped, duration, failedHooks = 0) {
   236	    let style = colors.bgGreen
   237	    let msg = ` ${passed || 0} passed`
   238	    let status = style.bold('  OK ')
   239	    if (failed) {
   240	      style = style.bgRed
   241	      status = style.bold('  FAIL ')
   242	      msg += `, ${failed} failed`
   243	    }
   244	
   245	    if (failedHooks > 0) {
   246	      style = style.bgRed
   247	      status = style.bold('  FAIL ')
   248	      msg += `, ${failedHooks} failedHooks`
   249	    }
   250	    status += style.grey(' |')
   251	
   252	    if (skipped) {
   253	      if (!failed) style = style.bgYellow
   254	      msg += `, ${skipped} skipped`
   255	    }
   256	    msg += '  '
   257	    print(status + style(msg) + colors.grey(` // ${duration}`))
   258	  },
   259	}
   260	
   261	function print(...msg) {
   262	  if (outputProcess) {
   263	    msg.unshift(outputProcess)
   264	  }
   265	  if (!newline) {
   266	    console.log()
   267	    newline = true
   268	  }
   269	
   270	  if (shouldMaskData()) {
   271	    msg = msg.map(item => (typeof item === 'string' ? maskData(item, getMaskConfig()) : item))
   272	  }
   273	
   274	  console.log.apply(this, msg)
   275	}
   276	
   277	function truncate(msg, gap = 0) {
   278	  if (msg.indexOf('\n') > 0 || outputLevel >= 3) {
   279	    return msg // don't cut multi line steps or on verbose log level
   280	  }
   281	  const width = (process.stdout.columns || 200) - gap - 4
   282	  if (msg.length > width) {
   283	    msg = msg.substr(0, width - 1) + figures.ellipsis
   284	  }
   285	  return msg
   286	}
   287

   106	  step(step) {

   119	      stepLine = colors.dim(truncate(stepLine, this.spaceShift))

diff --git a/lib/utils/mask_data.js b/lib/utils/mask_data.js
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..fd016105
--- /dev/null
+++ b/lib/utils/mask_data.js
@@ -0,0 +1,82 @@
+const { maskSensitiveData } = require('invisi-data')
+
+/**
+ * Mask sensitive data utility for CodeceptJS.
+ *
+ * Supports backward-compatible boolean configuration and object configuration
+ * with custom invisi-data patterns:
+ *
+ * maskSensitiveData: true
+ * maskSensitiveData: { enabled: true, patterns: [{ regex: /.../, mask: '...' }] }
+ *
+ * @param {string} input
+ * @param {boolean|object} config
+ * @returns {string}
+ */
+function maskData(input, config = getMaskConfig()) {
+  if (!shouldMaskData(config) || typeof input !== 'string' || input.trim().length === 0) {
+    return input
+  }
+
+  if (config === true) {
+    return maskSensitiveData(input)
+  }
+
+  return maskSensitiveData(input, normalizePatterns(config.patterns || []))
+}
+
+/**
+ * @returns {boolean|object}
+ */
+function getMaskConfig() {
+  return global.maskSensitiveData || false
+}
+
+/**
+ * @param {boolean|object} config
+ * @returns {boolean}
+ */
+function shouldMaskData(config = getMaskConfig()) {
+  return config === true || (typeof config === 'object' && config !== null && config.enabled !== false)
+}
+
+/**
+ * Convert string regex definitions to RegExp objects while keeping existing
+ * RegExp-based invisi-data patterns intact.
+ *
+ * @param {Array} patterns
+ * @returns {Array}
+ */
+function normalizePatterns(patterns) {
+  if (!Array.isArray(patterns)) return []
+
+  return patterns.map(pattern => {
+    if (!pattern || typeof pattern !== 'object' || pattern.regex instanceof RegExp) return pattern
+    if (typeof pattern.regex !== 'string') return pattern
+
+    return {
+      ...pattern,
+      regex: stringToRegExp(pattern.regex),
+    }
+  })
+}
+
+/**
+ * Accept either a plain regex source or JavaScript-like /source/flags notation.
+ *
+ * @param {string} value
+ * @returns {RegExp|string}
+ */
+function stringToRegExp(value) {
+  const match = value.match(/^\/(.*)\/([a-z]*)$/i)
+  if (!match) return new RegExp(value, 'g')
+
+  return new RegExp(match[1], match[2])
+}
+
+module.exports = {
+  maskData,
+  getMaskConfig,
+  shouldMaskData,
+  normalizePatterns,
+}

const fs=require('fs'), path=require('path'), zlib=require('zlib');
const repo='/testbed';
function readRef(ref){
  const p=path.join(repo,'.git',ref);
  if (fs.existsSync(p)) return fs.readFileSync(p,'utf8').trim();
  const packed=fs.readFileSync(path.join(repo,'.git','packed-refs'),'utf8');
  for (const line of packed.split(/\n/)) {
    if (!line || line[0]==='#' || line[0]==='^') continue;
    const [sha, name]=line.split(' ');
    if (name===ref) return sha;
  }
  throw new Error('ref not found '+ref);
}
function headSha(){
  const head=fs.readFileSync(path.join(repo,'.git','HEAD'),'utf8').trim();
  if (head.startsWith('ref: ')) return readRef(head.slice(5));
  return head;
}
function readObject(sha){
  const p=path.join(repo,'.git','objects',sha.slice(0,2),sha.slice(2));
  if (!fs.existsSync(p)) throw new Error('loose object not found '+sha);
  const buf=zlib.inflateSync(fs.readFileSync(p));
  const nul=buf.indexOf(0);
  const header=buf.slice(0,nul).toString();
  const body=buf.slice(nul+1);
  return { type: header.split(' ')[0], body };
}
function parseTree(body){
  const entries=[]; let i=0;
  while (i<body.length){
    const sp=body.indexOf(0x20,i); const mode=body.slice(i,sp).toString();
    const nul=body.indexOf(0,sp+1); const name=body.slice(sp+1,nul).toString();
    const sha=body.slice(nul+1,nul+21).toString('hex');
    entries.push({mode,name,sha}); i=nul+21;
  }
  return entries;
}
function getFile(filePath){
  const commit=readObject(headSha());
  const text=commit.body.toString();
  const treeSha=text.match(/^tree ([0-9a-f]{40})/m)[1];
  let sha=treeSha, parts=filePath.split('/');
  for (const part of parts){
    const obj=readObject(sha);
    if (obj.type !== 'tree') throw new Error('not tree');
    const entry=parseTree(obj.body).find(e=>e.name===part);
    if (!entry) throw new Error('missing '+part);
    sha=entry.sha;
  }
  const blob=readObject(sha);
  if (blob.type !== 'blob') throw new Error('not blob');
  return blob.body;
}
fs.writeFileSync(path.join(repo,'docs/plugins.md'), getFile('docs/plugins.md'));
console.log('restored docs/plugins.md from HEAD');
NODE

const fs=require('fs'), zlib=require('zlib'), path=require('path');
const repo='/testbed';
function indexSha(filepath){
 const b=fs.readFileSync(path.join(repo,'.git','index')); if(b.slice(0,4).toString()!=='DIRC') throw Error('bad'); const n=b.readUInt32BE(8); let off=12;
 for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
  const start=off; const sha=b.slice(off+40,off+60).toString('hex'); const flags=b.readUInt16BE(off+60); off+=62;
  const end=b.indexOf(0,off); const name=b.slice(off,end).toString(); off=end+1; while((off-start)%8) off++;
  if(name===filepath) return sha;
 }
}
function readIdx(idxPath){
 const b=fs.readFileSync(idxPath); let off=0; if(b.readUInt32BE(0)!==0xff744f63) throw Error('idx v1 unsupported'); off=8; const fan=[]; for(let i=0;i<256;i++) fan.push(b.readUInt32BE(off+i*4)); off+=1024; const n=fan[255]; const shas=[]; for(let i=0;i<n;i++) shas.push(b.slice(off+i*20,off+i*20+20).toString('hex')); off+=n*20; off+=n*4; const offsets=[]; const large=[]; for(let i=0;i<n;i++){ const v=b.readUInt32BE(off+i*4); if(v&0x80000000) { offsets.push(null); large.push({i,idx:v&0x7fffffff}); } else offsets.push(v); } off+=n*4; for (const item of large) { offsets[item.i] = Number(b.readBigUInt64BE(off+item.idx*8)); }
 return {shas, offsets};
}
const idxPath=path.join(repo,'.git/objects/pack/pack-8c90be908a4b16c84450258f1b728efe1ebfc0a3.idx');
const packPath=idxPath.replace(/\.idx$/,'.pack');
const idx=readIdx(idxPath); const sha=indexSha('docs/plugins.md'); console.log('sha',sha); const i=idx.shas.indexOf(sha); console.log('idx',i,'offset',idx.offsets[i]);
const sorted=[...idx.offsets].sort((a,b)=>a-b); const packSize=fs.statSync(packPath).size; function nextOffset(o){ for(const x of sorted){ if(x>o) return x;} return packSize-20; }
const pack=fs.readFileSync(packPath);
function parseHeader(o){ let c=pack[o++]; let type=(c>>4)&7; let size=c&15; let shift=4; while(c&0x80){ c=pack[o++]; size|=(c&0x7f)<<shift; shift+=7;} return {type,size,pos:o}; }
function inflateAt(pos,end){ return zlib.inflateSync(pack.slice(pos,end)); }
function readObjectAt(o){ const h=parseHeader(o); let pos=h.pos; const end=nextOffset(o); if(h.type===6){ let c=pack[pos++]; let val=c&0x7f; while(c&0x80){ c=pack[pos++]; val=((val+1)<<7)|(c&0x7f); } const baseOff=o-val; const delta=inflateAt(pos,end); const base=readObjectAt(baseOff); return applyDelta(base,delta); }

 return {type:h.type, data:inflateAt(pos,end)};
}
function readVar(buf, st){ let res=0, shift=0, c; do { c=buf[st.i++]; res|=(c&0x7f)<<shift; shift+=7; } while(c&0x80); return res; }
function applyDelta(baseObj, delta){ const st={i:0}; const baseSize=readVar(delta,st); const resSize=readVar(delta,st); const out=[]; while(st.i<delta.length){ const op=delta[st.i++]; if(op&0x80){ let cpOff=0, cpSize=0; if(op&1) cpOff=delta[st.i++]; if(op&2) cpOff|=delta[st.i++]<<8; if(op&4) cpOff|=delta[st.i++]<<16; if(op&8) cpOff|=delta[st.i++]<<24; if(op&0x10) cpSize=delta[st.i++]; if(op&0x20) cpSize|=delta[st.i++]<<8; if(op&0x40) cpSize|=delta[st.i++]<<16; if(cpSize===0) cpSize=0x10000; out.push(baseObj.data.slice(cpOff, cpOff+cpSize)); } else if(op){ out.push(delta.slice(st.i, st.i+op)); st.i+=op; } else throw Error('bad delta'); }
 const data=Buffer.concat(out); if(data.length!==resSize) console.error('size mismatch', data.length,resSize); return {type:baseObj.type, data}; }

 #### Configuration
 
-- `clusterize` (number) - minimum number of failures to trigger clustering analysis. Default: 5
-- `analyze` (number) - maximum number of individual test failures to analyze in detail. Default: 2
-- `vision` (boolean) - enables visual analysis of test screenshots. Default: false
-- `categories` (array) - list of failure categories for classification. Defaults to:
-  - Browser connection error / browser crash
-  - Network errors (server error, timeout, etc)
-  - HTML / page elements (not found, not visible, etc)
-  - Navigation errors (404, etc)
-  - Code errors (syntax error, JS errors, etc)
-  - Library & framework errors
-  - Data errors (password incorrect, invalid format, etc)
-  - Assertion failures

diff --git a/lib/utils/mask_data.js b/lib/utils/mask_data.js
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..fd016105
--- /dev/null
+++ b/lib/utils/mask_data.js
@@ -0,0 +1,82 @@
+const { maskSensitiveData } = require('invisi-data')
+
+/**
+ * Mask sensitive data utility for CodeceptJS.
+ *
+ * Supports backward-compatible boolean configuration and object configuration
+ * with custom invisi-data patterns:
+ *
+ * maskSensitiveData: true
+ * maskSensitiveData: { enabled: true, patterns: [{ regex: /.../, mask: '...' }] }
+ *
+ * @param {string} input
+ * @param {boolean|object} config
+ * @returns {string}
+ */
+function maskData(input, config = getMaskConfig()) {
+  if (!shouldMaskData(config) || typeof input !== 'string' || input.trim().length === 0) {
+    return input
+  }
+
+  if (config === true) {
+    return maskSensitiveData(input)
+  }
+
+  return maskSensitiveData(input, normalizePatterns(config.patterns || []))
+}
+
+/**
+ * @returns {boolean|object}
+ */
+function getMaskConfig() {
+  return global.maskSensitiveData || false
+}
+
+/**
+ * @param {boolean|object} config
+ * @returns {boolean}
+ */
+function shouldMaskData(config = getMaskConfig()) {
+  return config === true || (typeof config === 'object' && config !== null && config.enabled !== false)
+}
+
+/**
+ * Convert string regex definitions to RegExp objects while keeping existing
+ * RegExp-based invisi-data patterns intact.
+ *
+ * @param {Array} patterns
+ * @returns {Array}
+ */
+function normalizePatterns(patterns) {
+  if (!Array.isArray(patterns)) return []
+
+  return patterns.map(pattern => {
+    if (!pattern || typeof pattern !== 'object' || pattern.regex instanceof RegExp) return pattern
+    if (typeof pattern.regex !== 'string') return pattern
+
+    return {
+      ...pattern,
+      regex: stringToRegExp(pattern.regex),
+    }
+  })
+}
+
+/**
+ * Accept either a plain regex source or JavaScript-like /source/flags notation.
+ *
+ * @param {string} value
+ * @returns {RegExp|string}
+ */
+function stringToRegExp(value) {
+  const match = value.match(/^\/(.*)\/([a-z]*)$/i)
+  if (!match) return new RegExp(value, 'g')
+
+  return new RegExp(match[1], match[2])
+}
+
+module.exports = {
+  maskData,
+  getMaskConfig,
+  shouldMaskData,
+  normalizePatterns,
+}

diff --git a/lib/utils/mask_data.js b/lib/utils/mask_data.js
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..fd016105
--- /dev/null
+++ b/lib/utils/mask_data.js
@@ -0,0 +1,82 @@
+const { maskSensitiveData } = require('invisi-data')
+
+/**
+ * Mask sensitive data utility for CodeceptJS.
+ *
+ * Supports backward-compatible boolean configuration and object configuration
+ * with custom invisi-data patterns:
+ *
+ * maskSensitiveData: true
+ * maskSensitiveData: { enabled: true, patterns: [{ regex: /.../, mask: '...' }] }
+ *
+ * @param {string} input
+ * @param {boolean|object} config
+ * @returns {string}
+ */
+function maskData(input, config = getMaskConfig()) {
+  if (!shouldMaskData(config) || typeof input !== 'string' || input.trim().length === 0) {
+    return input
+  }
+
+  if (config === true) {
+    return maskSensitiveData(input)
+  }
+
+  return maskSensitiveData(input, normalizePatterns(config.patterns || []))
+}
+
+/**
+ * @returns {boolean|object}
+ */
+function getMaskConfig() {
+  return global.maskSensitiveData || false
+}
+
+/**
+ * @param {boolean|object} config
+ * @returns {boolean}
+ */
+function shouldMaskData(config = getMaskConfig()) {
+  return config === true || (typeof config === 'object' && config !== null && config.enabled !== false)
+}
+
+/**
+ * Convert string regex definitions to RegExp objects while keeping existing
+ * RegExp-based invisi-data patterns intact.
+ *
+ * @param {Array} patterns
+ * @returns {Array}
+ */
+function normalizePatterns(patterns) {
+  if (!Array.isArray(patterns)) return []
+
+  return patterns.map(pattern => {
+    if (!pattern || typeof pattern !== 'object' || pattern.regex instanceof RegExp) return pattern
+    if (typeof pattern.regex !== 'string') return pattern
+
+    return {
+      ...pattern,
+      regex: stringToRegExp(pattern.regex),
+    }
+  })
+}
+
+/**
+ * Accept either a plain regex source or JavaScript-like /source/flags notation.
+ *
+ * @param {string} value
+ * @returns {RegExp|string}
+ */
+function stringToRegExp(value) {
+  const match = value.match(/^\/(.*)\/([a-z]*)$/i)
+  if (!match) return new RegExp(value, 'g')
+
+  return new RegExp(match[1], match[2])
+}
+
+module.exports = {
+  maskData,
+  getMaskConfig,
+  shouldMaskData,
+  normalizePatterns,
+}
